 ) Skandmata is worshiped on the fifth day of Navratri (navratri 2019)
 skandamata ko vatsalya kii murti mana jaataa he

 ek baar jab yah sabhi pareekshanon safaltaapurvak ho jaaenge, to desi parmaanu ghadi kaa prayog experimental nevigation upgrah par antariksh main isaki sateekta or sthayitv kaa pareekshan karne ke liye kiya jayega
 The SAC director said, "with the development of the indigenous atomic clock, ISRO has become one of the few space organizations in the world that has the ability to develop this highly sophisticated technology
 ham emport kari hui parmaanu ghadi ke dizin or technology ke bare me itnaa nahin jaanate hai
 But Desi Watch is developed based on our design and specifications
 yah ghadi emported ke rup main utani hi acchhee he

 'bhartiya kshetreenevigation satellite system(iareneses) yaa navich ke hisse ke rup main pehle launch kiye gaye sabhi saat nevigation upgrahon main teen aaayaatit rubium parmaanu ghadiyon hai
 On the functioning of these atomic clocks, Tapan Mishra said, 'all the seven satellites launched earlier have synchronized (synchronized) atomic clocks
 alag-alag kakshaon main sthit vibhinn upgrahon ke parmaanu ghadiyon ke bich kaa samay antar ek nevigation resiver yaa prithvi par ek vastu kii sateek sthiti ko maapne ke liye upyog kiya jaataa he
 If there are any flaws in the atomic clock, or the time difference between it and the other clocks is not accurate, it in turn provides the wrong position of the object
 parmaanu ghadiyon ke alaava, ek nevigation upgrah main crystal ghadiyon bhi hote hai lekin ve parmaanu ghadiyon ke rup main sateek nahin hai

 'isro main ek vishwasaneey strot ke anusaar, launch kiye gaye saat nevigation upgrahon main se kuch main istemaal kiye gaye 21 parmaanu ghadiyon main se nau erar dikhaa rahe hai

 ye byaap upgrah, jinke paas swadeshi parmaanu ghadiyon bhi hone kii sambhaavna he, ve desi jeepies system main bafer jod denge

 'pichley maheene 12 april ko, isro ne bharat ke pehle nevigation upgrah iareneses-1 e ko badalane ke liye safaltaapurvak nausena iareneses-1 ai launch kiya, jinke teen parmaanu ghadiyon ne do saal pehle kaam karnaa band kar diya tha
